  postgres:
    image: postgres:16-alpine
    container_name: postgres
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: midpoint
      POSTGRES_USER: midpointuser
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: P0stgr3sS3cur32026!
    volumes:
      - ./data/postgres:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U midpointuser -d midpoint"]
      interval: 5s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  midpoint:
    image: evolveum/midpoint:4.9
    container_name: midpoint
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    volumes:
      - ./data/midpoint:/opt/midpoint/var
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
    environment:
      REPODATABASETYPE: postgresql
      REPOJDBCURL: jdbc:postgresql://postgres:5432/midpoint?user=midpointuser&password=P0stgr3sS3cur32026!
      JAVA_OPTS: -Xms512m -Xmx1024m -Dfile.encoding=UTF-8
      MPKEYSTOREPASSWORD: midpointkeystore2026
      MP_SET_midpoint_administrator_initialPassword: M1dP0!ntAdm!n2026
EOF

paulo@iga-gf-02:~/midpoint-deploy$ # Valida o número de tabelas
TABLE_COUNT=$(docker exec postgres psql -U midpointuser -d midpoint -t -c "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM information_schema.tables WHERE table_schema='public'")
echo "Tabelas criadas: $TABLE_COUNT"
Tabelas criadas:    101
paulo@iga-gf-02:~/midpoint-deploy$
paulo@iga-gf-02:~/midpoint-deploy$
paulo@iga-gf-02:~/midpoint-deploy$
paulo@iga-gf-02:~/midpoint-deploy$
paulo@iga-gf-02:~/midpoint-deploy$ # Se o número for >=85, sobe o midPoint
if [ "$TABLE_COUNT" -ge 85 ]; then
    echo "✅ Número de tabelas OK. Subindo o midPoint..."
    docker compose up -d midpoint
    echo "Aguardando inicialização (60s)..."
    sleep 60
    echo "=== Verificando log ==="
    docker logs midpoint 2>&1 | grep "Database schema is compliant"
    echo "=== Testando HTTP ==="
    curl -I http://localhost:8080/midpoint
else
    echo "❌ ERRO: Apenas $TABLE_COUNT tabelas. Esperado >=85."
    exit 1
fi
